%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%功能求出矩阵train_total中A列中各个元素出现的次数%%%%%%
hanglie = size(train_total)
 hangshu=hanglie(1,1)  %总数据的行数
 lieshu=hanglie(1,2)       %总数据的列数


A=train_total(:,42)
Azhongleixing=unique(A)


hanglieAlei= size(Azhongleixing)
 hangshuAlei=hanglieAlei(1,1)
 lieshuAlei=hanglieAlei(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr=[];                
for m=1: hangshuAlei
     j=0
    for i=1:hangshu
        if train_total(i,42) == Azhongleixing(m,1)
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr(m)=j
    end
end

train_data1_1lie=train_data1(:,1)
train_data1_1liezhongleixing=unique(train_data1_1lie)

hanglietrain_data1_1lie= size(train_data1_1liezhongleixing)
hangshutrain_data1_1lie=hanglietrain_data1_1lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data1_1lie=hanglietrain_data1_1lie(1,2)



hanglietrain_data1= size(train_data1)
train_data1_hangshu=hanglietrain_data1(1,1)
train_data1_lieshu=hanglietrain_data1(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data1_1lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
     j=0;
    for i=1:train_data1_hangshu
        if train_data1(i,1) == train_data1_1liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data1_1lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data1_1lie' %%转置
result_train_data1_1lie = [train_data1_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_1lie'];

train_data1_1lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
       train_data1_1lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data1_1lie(m)/train_data1_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data1_1lie = [train_data1_1liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_1lie',train_data1_1lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data1_1lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data1_sumshang1= 0;
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_1lie
       train_data1_1lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data1_1lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data1_1lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data1_sumshang1= train_data1_sumshang1+  train_data1_1lie_xinxishang(m);
end

hangshutrain_data1_23lie=hanglietrain_data1_23lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data1_23lie=hanglietrain_data1_23lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data1_23lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_23lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data1_hangshu
        if train_data1(i,23) == train_data1_23liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data1_23lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data1_23lie' %%转置
result_train_data1_23lie = [train_data1_23liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_23lie'];

train_data1_23lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_23lie
       train_data1_23lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data1_23lie(m)/train_data1_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data1_23lie = [train_data1_23liezhongleixing,arr_train_data1_23lie',train_data1_23lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data1_23lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data1_sumshang23 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data1_23lie
       train_data1_23lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data1_23lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data1_23lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data1_sumshang23 = train_data1_sumshang23 +  train_data1_23lie_xinxishang(m);
end

train_data2_19lie=train_data2(:,19)
train_data2_19liezhongleixing=unique(train_data2_19lie)


hanglietrain_data2_19lie= size(train_data2_19liezhongleixing)
hangshutrain_data2_19lie=hanglietrain_data2_19lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data2_19lie=hanglietrain_data2_19lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data2_19lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_19lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data2_hangshu
        if train_data2(i,19) == train_data2_19liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data2_19lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data2_19lie' %%转置
result_train_data2_19lie = [train_data2_19liezhongleixing,arr_train_data2_19lie'];

train_data2_19lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_19lie
       train_data2_19lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data2_19lie(m)/train_data2_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data2_19lie = [train_data2_19liezhongleixing,arr_train_data2_19lie',train_data2_19lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data2_19lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data2_sumshang19 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data2_19lie
       train_data2_19lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data2_19lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data2_19lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data2_sumshang19 = train_data2_sumshang19 +  train_data2_19lie_xinxishang(m);
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出 traindata1的第2列的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

train_data3_15liezhongleixing=unique(train_data3_15lie)


hanglietrain_data3_15lie= size(train_data3_15liezhongleixing)
hangshutrain_data3_15lie=hanglietrain_data3_15lie(1,1)
lieshutrain_data3_15lie=hanglietrain_data3_15lie(1,2)

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%arr存储A中各个类型出现的次数%%%%%%%%%%%
arr_train_data3_15lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_15lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data3_hangshu
        if train_data3(i,15) == train_data3_15liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data3_15lie(m)=j;
    end
end

arr_train_data3_15lie' %%转置
result_train_data3_15lie = [train_data3_15liezhongleixing,arr_train_data3_15lie'];

train_data3_15lie_bili = [];
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_15lie
       train_data3_15lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data3_15lie(m)/train_data3_hangshu;
end

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%第三列数据太小了 不能一起存%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
result_train_data3_15lie = [train_data3_15liezhongleixing,arr_train_data3_15lie',train_data3_15lie_bili'];

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%求出了traindata1的第1列数据的信息熵%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
train_data3_15lie_xinxishang= [];
train_data3_sumshang15 =0
for m=1: hangshutrain_data3_15lie
       train_data3_15lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data3_15lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data3_15lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data3_sumshang15 = train_data3_sumshang15 +  train_data3_15lie_xinxishang(m);
end

arr_train_data4_11lie=[];                
for m=1: hangshutrain_data4_11lie
     j=0;;
    for i=1:train_data4_hangshu
        if train_data4(i,11) == train_data4_11liezhongleixing(m,1);
         j=j+1;
     end
        arr_train_data4_11lie(m)=j;
    end
end

       train_data4_11lie_bili(m) = arr_train_data4_11lie(m)/train_data4_hangshu;
end

       train_data4_11lie_xinxishang(m) = -train_data4_11lie_bili(m)*log2(train_data4_11lie_bili(m)) ;
       train_data4_sumshang11 = train_data4_sumshang11 +  train_data4_11lie_xinxishang(m);

        bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(1) =1;

        bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(1) = 1000*result_train_data1_1lie(j,3);
        break;
   end

        bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(38) = 1000*result_train_data1_38lie(j,3);
        break;
   end
end

   end

        k=i;
     end
    end


   test_data_jieguo_hangshu(n) = 400+k;
